 2021 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      6 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | * draws sprites via direct-page writes to SHR shadow RAM.

 2023 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      8 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | * Call: copy sprite table ($18 bytes) to bank $00 direct page,
 2024 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      9 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | *       LDA #dp_address / JSR Create_Sprite
 2025 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     10 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | *
 2026 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     11 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | * Sprite table format (24 bytes at DP offsets $00-$17):
 2027 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     12 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | *   $00 ADRL Rout_Adr    — output: where compiled code is written
 2028 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     13 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | *   $04 ADRL Shape_Adr   — input: shape pixel data (24-bit)
 2029 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     14 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | *   $08 ADRL Msk_Adr     — $000000=none, $FFFF00=auto, $FEFE00=decor

 2031 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     16 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | *   $0E DA   Nb_Lgn      — bytes per shape row
 2032 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     17 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | *   $10 DA   Nb_Col      — bytes per shape column
 2033 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     18 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | *   $12 DA   Lgn         — row ($FFFF=dynamic via Y register)
 2034 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     19 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D84               | *   $14 DA   Col         — column
